About Medical Care in Palm Beach County

Palm Beach County, Florida is home to 5237 verified medical professionals spanning 32 specialties. The county's healthcare landscape includes specialists in Internal Medicine, Family Medicine, Psychiatry, Anesthesiology, Emergency Medicine, ensuring residents have access to comprehensive medical care.

With doctors practicing in 150 cities across the county, including BOCA RATON, WEST PALM BEACH, DELRAY BEACH, patients can find quality healthcare close to home. 1501 doctors are also willing to travel, providing additional flexibility for patients with mobility challenges or those in underserved areas.

All doctors listed on EliteMD are verified through the National Provider Identifier (NPI) Registry, ensuring accurate credentials and practice information. Our directory helps patients make informed decisions when choosing a healthcare provider in Palm Beach County.

Frequently Asked Questions

How many doctors are in Palm Beach County, Florida?
EliteMD lists 5237 verified medical professionals across 32 specialties in Palm Beach County, Florida. This includes specialists in Internal Medicine, Family Medicine, Psychiatry, and more.
What are the top medical specialties in Palm Beach County?
The most represented specialties in Palm Beach County are Internal Medicine (1013 doctors), Family Medicine (642 doctors), Psychiatry (433 doctors), Anesthesiology (284 doctors), Emergency Medicine (247 doctors).
Which cities in Palm Beach County have the most doctors?
The cities with the most doctors in Palm Beach County are BOCA RATON (958), WEST PALM BEACH (734), DELRAY BEACH (540), BOYNTON BEACH (505), JUPITER (367).
How are doctors in Palm Beach County verified?
All doctors on EliteMD are verified through the National Provider Identifier (NPI) Registry, a federal database maintained by the Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services. Each doctor's credentials, specialty, and practice location are confirmed through official records.
Can I find a specialist who will travel to Palm Beach County?
Yes, many specialists on EliteMD are available to travel. Use the "Will Travel" filter on the search page to find doctors willing to come to Palm Beach County for consultations and procedures.
